G                1673 syn/syntax.c   YY_RULE(int) yy_arg_type(GREG *G)
G                1675 syn/syntax.c     int yypos0= G->pos, yythunkpos0= G->thunkpos;
G                1677 syn/syntax.c     yyText(G, G->begin, G->end);
G                1680 syn/syntax.c       int yypos2= G->pos, yythunkpos2= G->thunkpos;
G                1681 syn/syntax.c       if (!yymatchChar(G, 's')) goto l3;
G                1684 syn/syntax.c       G->pos= yypos2; G->thunkpos= yythunkpos2;
G                1685 syn/syntax.c       if (!yymatchChar(G, 'S')) goto l4;
G                1688 syn/syntax.c       G->pos= yypos2; G->thunkpos= yythunkpos2;
G                1689 syn/syntax.c       if (!yymatchChar(G, 'n')) goto l5;
G                1692 syn/syntax.c       G->pos= yypos2; G->thunkpos= yythunkpos2;
